The game and its variants are popular in many countries and under various names.\r\n\r\nParchisi originated in India by the 6th century. \r\n\r\nEach player rolls the die; the highest roller begins the game. Players alternate turns in a clockwise direction.\r\n\r\nLudo can be played by two, three, or four, without partnerships. To enter a token into play from its yard to its starting square, a player must roll a 6. If the player has no tokens yet in play and rolls other than a 6, the turn passes to the next player. Once a player has one or more tokens in play, he selects a token and moves it forwards along the track the number of squares indicated by the dice. Players must always move a token according to the die value rolled. Passes are not allowed; if no move is possible, the turn moves to the next player.\r\n\r\nPlayers may not end their move on a square they already occupy. If the advance of a token ends on a square occupied by an opponent's token, the opponent token is returned to its owner's yard. Dealer gives 13 cards to each player. Initiating a game by throwing a single card of any suit the other players also follow the same suit unless they runs out of that particular suit. Absence of identical suit allows player to throw a card of another suit and the current round is won by highest card. Trump cards can be used to conquer other cards when no more cards of the same suit are there to offer. Trump card is by default Spade but you can set different trump suit like club, diamond or heart in this Call Break tash game.\r\n\r\nCall Break the term \"hand\" is used instead of trick, and \"Call\" is used instead of bid. After each deal player have to make a \"Call\" or \"bid\" for the number of hands he/she can capture, and the objective is to capture at least that many hand in a round, and try to break other player i.e. stop them from getting their Call. After each round, points will be calculated. \r\n\r\nCallbreak hearts card game is also known as Lakadi or lakdi in various part of India. In Bangladesh Call Break card game is also known as Call Bridge, Ghochi or locha.\r\n\r\nCallbreak spades bridge game Rules :-\r\n• Dealer distributes each player 13 cards.\r\n• After distribution of cards, players have to make bid.\r\n• Player who bid first, he will throw the first card.\r\n• Next player should throw the card of greater value than previous card of same suit.\r\n• If player does not have greater value of card then he can throw any card of same suit. \r\n• If player does not have same suit then he can throw the trump card.\r\n• If player does not have same suit and trump card then he can throw card of any suit.\r\n• The highest priority card wins the hand and gets point.\r\n• If player not able to get points equals to his bid, then he will get minus points equal to his bid.\r\n\r\nCallbreak hearts card game Features :-\r\n• Beautiful animations and Graphics.\r\n• Instead of playing Five Rounds you can select Number of Round.\r\n• You don't required Internet connection to play against computer(Bots)\r\n• You can set different trump suit like club, diamond, heart or Spade.\r\n• Various table and card deck to choose from.\r\n• Fast paced game play.\r\n• Simple and addictive UI Design and easy settings.\r\n\r\nCall break card game is also very much popular in North America as Spades.
